Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Springfield, MO, February 5, 2025</b><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> &#8211; </font>O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221; or &#8220;O&#8217;Reilly&#8221;) (<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Nasdaq: &#160;</font>ORLY), a leading retailer in the automotive aftermarket industry, today announced record revenue for its fourth quarter and full-year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024. &#160;The results represent 32 consecutive years of comparable store sales growth and record revenue and operating income for O&#8217;Reilly since becoming a public company in April of 1993. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">4</font><sup style="font-size:8.25pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:top;">th</sup><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> Quarter Financial Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Brad Beckham, O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s CEO, commented, &#8220;We are pleased to report a strong finish to 2024 in the fourth quarter, highlighted by 4.4% growth in comparable store sales, driven by solid growth in both professional and DIY. &#160;Our Team is relentlessly focused on executing our industry-leading model at a high level, which we believe continues to generate market share gains on both sides of our business. &#160;I would like to take this opportunity to commend Team O&#8217;Reilly on their performance in the fourth quarter and thank each of you for your hard work and continued commitment to providing excellent customer service.&#8221;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Sales for the fourth quarter ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, increased $264 million, or 7%, to $4.10 billion from $3.83 billion for the same period one year ago. &#160;Gross profit for the fourth quarter increased 7% to $2.10 billion (or 51.3% of sales) from $1.97 billion (or 51.3% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Selling, general and administrative expenses (&#8220;SG&amp;A&#8221;) for the fourth quarter increased 9% to $1.36 billion (or 33.3% of sales) from $1.25 billion (or 32.6% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Operating income for the fourth quarter increased 3% to $739 million (or 18.0% of sales) from $719 million (or 18.8% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">SG&amp;A expenses for the fourth quarter included a charge of $35 million to adjust reserves relating to our self-insurance liabilities for historic auto liability claims. &#160;The adjustment relates to claims that occurred prior to 2024 and reflects adverse claim development experience and revised assumptions used to estimate future liabilities for these claim years.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Net income for the fourth quarter ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, decreased $1 million to $551 million (or 13.5% of sales) from $553 million (or 14.4% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Diluted earnings per common share for the fourth quarter increased 3% to $9.50 on 58 million shares versus $9.26 on 60 million shares for the same period one year ago. &#160;The self-insurance reserve adjustment, net of tax, impacted fourth quarter net income and diluted earnings per share by $27 million and $0.46, respectively.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Full-Year Financial Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Mr. Beckham continued, &#8220;Our strong performance in the fourth quarter lifted our full-year comparable store sales growth to 2.9%, at the high end of our revised guidance range of 2% to 3%. &#160;While our 2024 results were below our expectations entering the year, we are pleased with our Team&#8217;s ability to deliver solid comparable store sales growth despite tough market conditions. &#160;2024 represents our 32nd consecutive year of annual comparable store sales growth and record earnings, and I </p></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:center;margin:24pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div></div><hr style="background-color:#000000;clear:both;color:#000000;height:2pt;line-height:0;margin-bottom:30pt;margin-left:5.88%;margin-right:5.88%;margin-top:30pt;page-break-after:always;width:88.24%;border-width:0;"><div style="max-width:100%;padding-left:5.88%;padding-right:5.88%;position:relative;"><div style="clear:both;max-width:100%;position:relative;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">want to congratulate Team O&#8217;Reilly on their consistent performance and unwavering commitment to our customers. &#160;Our Team also delivered a strong finish to our expansion efforts in 2024, meeting our new store opening target with the successful opening of 198 net, new stores and completing our planned distribution expansion with the relocation of our Atlanta, Georgia distribution center to a larger, modern facility in the fourth quarter.&#8221;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Sales for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, increased $896 million, or 6%, to $16.71 billion from $15.81 billion for the same period one year ago. &#160;Gross profit for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, increased 6% to $8.55 billion (or 51.2% of sales) from $8.10 billion (or 51.3% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;SG&amp;A for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, increased 8% to $5.30 billion (or 31.7% of sales) from $4.92 billion (or 31.1% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Operating income for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, increased 2% to $3.25 billion (or 19.5% of sales) from $3.19 billion (or 20.2% of sales) for the same period one year ago.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Net income for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, increased $40 million, or 2%, to $2.39 billion (or 14.3% of sales) from $2.35 billion (or 14.8% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Diluted earnings per common share for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, increased 6% to $40.66 on 59 million shares versus $38.47 on 61 million shares for the same period one year ago.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">4</font><sup style="font-size:8.25pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:top;">th</sup><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> Quarter and Full-Year Comparable Store Sales Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Comparable store sales are calculated based on the change in sales for U.S. stores open at least one year and exclude sales of specialty machinery, sales to independent parts stores, and sales to Team Members, as well as sales from Leap Day for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024. &#160;Online sales for ship-to-home orders and pick-up-in-store orders for U.S. stores open at least one year are included in the comparable store sales calculation. &#160;Comparable store sales increased 4.4% for the fourth quarter ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, on top of 3.4% for the same period one year ago. &#160;Comparable store sales increased 2.9% for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, on top of 7.9% for the same period one year ago. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Share Repurchase Program</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">During the fourth quarter ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024, the Company repurchased 0.4 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $1,207.43, for a total investment of $472 million. &#160;During the year ended December 31, 2024, the Company repurchased 1.9 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $1,072.47, for a total investment of $2.08 billion. &#160;Excise tax on shares repurchased, assessed at one percent of the fair market value of shares repurchased, was $20.8 million for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2024. &#160;Subsequent to the end of the fourth quarter and through the date of this release, the Company repurchased an additional 0.1 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $1,232.37, for a total investment of $181 million. &#160;The Company has repurchased a total of 96.2 million shares of its common stock under its share repurchase program since the inception of the program in January of 2011 and through the date of this release, at an average price of $264.49, for a total aggregate investment of $25.44 billion. &#160;As of the date of this release, the Company had approximately $2.31 billion remaining under its current share repurchase authorizations. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">This release contains certain financial information not derived in accordance with United States generally accepted accounting principles (&#8220;GAAP&#8221;). &#160;These items include adjusted debt to earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, amortization, share-based compensation, and rent (&#8220;EBITDAR&#8221;) and free cash flow. &#160;The Company does not, nor does it suggest investors should, consider such non-GAAP financial measures in isolation from, or as a substitute for, GAAP financial information. &#160;The Company believes that the presentation of adjusted debt to EBITDAR and free cash flow provide meaningful supplemental information to both management and investors that is indicative of the Company&#8217;s core operations. &#160;The Company has included a reconciliation of this additional information to the most comparable GAAP measure in the table above and the selected financial information below. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Earnings Conference Call Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">About O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc.</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc. was founded in 1957 by the O&#8217;Reilly family and is one of the largest specialty retailers of automotive aftermarket parts, tools, supplies, equipment, and accessories in the United States, serving both the do-it-yourself and professional service provider markets. &#160;Visit the Company&#8217;s website at www.OReillyAuto.com for additional information about O&#8217;Reilly, including access to online shopping and current promotions, store locations, hours and services, employment opportunities, and other programs. &#160;As of December&#160;31,&#160;2024, the Company operated 6,378 stores across 48 U.S. states, Puerto Rico, Mexico, and Canada. style="border-collapse:collapse;font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:3pt;table-layout:fixed;text-align:justify;width:100%;border:0pt;"><tr><td style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:6.75pt;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;width:18pt;padding:0pt;">(2)</td><td style="padding:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:9pt;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;">Calculated as inventory divided by store count at the end of the reported period.</font></td></tr></table><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="border-collapse:collapse;font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:3pt;table-layout:fixed;text-align:justify;width:100%;border:0pt;"><tr><td style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:6.75pt;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;width:18pt;padding:0pt;">(3)</td><td style="padding:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:9pt;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;">Calculated as accounts payable divided by inventory.</font></td></tr></table><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="border-collapse:collapse;font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:3pt;table-layout:fixed;text-align:justify;width:100%;border:0pt;"><tr><td style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:6.75pt;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;width:18pt;padding:0pt;">(4)</td><td style="padding:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:9pt;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;">Represents O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s U.S. and Puerto Rico operations only.</font></td></tr></table><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="border-collapse:collapse;font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:3pt;table-layout:fixed;text-align:justify;width:100%;border:0pt;"><tr><td style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:6.75pt;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;width:18pt;padding:0pt;">(5)</td><td style="padding:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:9pt;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;">Calculated as sales less jobber sales, divided by weighted-average square footage. &#160;Weighted-average square footage is determined by weighting store square footage based on the approximate dates of store openings, acquisitions, expansions, or closures.</font></td></tr></table><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="border-collapse:collapse;font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:3pt;table-layout:fixed;text-align:justify;width:100%;border:0pt;"><tr><td style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:6.75pt;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;width:18pt;padding:0pt;">(6)</td><td style="padding:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:9pt;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;">Calculated as sales less jobber sales, divided by weighted-average stores. &#160;Weighted-average stores is determined by weighting stores based on their approximate dates of openings, acquisitions, or closures.</font></td></tr></table></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:center;margin:24pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div></div><hr
